 desh ke sabhi 125 karod se adhik nagarikon ko ek unic biometric link idi number 'aadhaar' dena shuru hue abhi ek dashak bhi nahin hue hai
 This number has been given to 112 crore Indians
 is aadhaar program ko shuru karne ke peeche sarkaar kii manshaa desh ke sabhi nagarikon kii pahchaan kaa ek jariya taiyaar karnaa tha
 But now that the government is starting to use it to ease its functioning, it is estimated that its program is also facing the danger of becoming overly large
 idi kii chunauti?desh main kisi kaam ko karne ke liye idi kii samasya rahati he
 If you want a mobile SIM, give 2-3 ids
 driving license ke liye idi, passport ke liye idi
 Even if an institution or government asks for ID, you will disclose documents like Voter ID, Driving License, Ration Card
 lekin in sabhi document par sansthaaen to dur sarkaar tak sawaal khadaa kar detii he
 Therefore, to solve all these challenges, the central government has an Aadhaar number
 ise nagarikon kii aankh se unic retina image or fingerprint ke jariye taiyaar kiya jaataa he
 This number cannot be duplicated and is being implemented in ID country
 aadhaar kaa vistarbank acount se judane vaala nagarikon kaa aadhaar number sarkaar ke liye vittiya madad pahunchane kaa jariya banegaa
 Where previously only selected educated people could get the benefit of government schemes, which were aware of the use of ids, forms etc
 is aadhaar ke sahare sarkaar nagarikon ke bank khaaton main sidhe paisa transfar kar sakegi
 Where earlier a large section of the country was outside the scope of banking, with the help of Aadhaar, it can easily take services like health, PDS, Jan Dhan etc
 from the bank, insurance services as well as the government
 jarurat padane par aadhaar kii madad se kisi se udhaar lene, pension fund se paise nikaalane, railway or hawaii yatra ke liye tikat lene jaisi sevaaon ko bhi aasaani se kiya ja saktaa he
 For all these services, the government or institutions will only need to scan your fingerprint or eye and you will get the green signal for all services

 aadhaar number lenaa anivaary nahin hoga
 It will only be used to transfer the financial benefit given in the name of Social Security directly to the bank account of citizens
 lekin kendra sarkaar ke faislon se saaf he ki maujuuda samay main kendra sarkaar aadhaar ko sabhi sevaaon ke liye anivaary karne kii disha main aage bad rahe hai
